	  (mps && mps.insertAd && mps.insertAd('#dart_wrapper_badgea', 'badgea'));	
	});
</script>

                <h2 class="module-header tabTitle">
                	 
						'Binge' with Carl Quintanilla: Season One

            <div class="carouselBody" >
        <div class="leftArrow disabled">&lsaquo;</div>
            <ul><li><!-- new asset.tpl begin --><div  class="asset  cnbcvideo imgasset desc_size160_105">        <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" class="video-icon">
